				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Jesu, nun sei gepreiset, BWV 41 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1724 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Jesu, nun sei gepreiset
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">O Jesus, now be praised
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Translations
</th>
<td><span title="tr, ca, es">Jesu</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Name Aliases
</th>
<td><span title="fr">Jésus, sois loué</span>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Authorities
</th>
<td><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/identities/containsVIAFID/174969443">WorldCat</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jesu,_nun_sei_gepreiset,_BWV_41">Wikipedia</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_International_Authority_File" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Virtual International Authority File">VIAF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://viaf.org/viaf/174969443">174969443</a>; <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblioth%C3%A8que_nationale_de_France" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bibliothèque nationale de France">BNF</a>: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://catalogue.bnf.fr/ark:/12148/cb13909593h">13909593h</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 41&#160;; BC A 22
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 343
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>C major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements:
<ol><li> Chorus: Jesu, nun sei gepreiset (C&#160;major)
</li><li> Aria (soprano): Laß uns, o höchster Gott, das Jahr vollbringen (G&#160;major)
</li><li> Recitativo (alto): Ach! deine Hand, dein Segen muß allein (A&#160;minor-E&#160;minor)
</li><li> Aria (tenor): Woferne du den edlen Frieden (A&#160;minor)
</li><li> Recitativo (bass): Doch weil der Feind bei Tag und Nacht (C&#160;major)
</li><li> Chorale: Dein ist allein die Ehre (C&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1724 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1725-01-01 in Leipzig (1st Performance)<br />1732-35 (2nd Performance)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1860 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>

</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
